SENTIENT SPECIES:
Four-Armed Robots with Giant Eyes: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have four arms. They have bilateral symmetry. Their giant eyes take up most of their head. They are meditative and deeply rationalist. They were created by the Third Republic of Antoids and Catoids on Gykop I as servants in 1064.
	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: 1 CON: 1 INT: 2 CHA: 0
Tiny Red Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have red skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are modest and deeply rationalist. They were created by the Third Empire of Tiny Robots on Mycon III as servants in 927.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 2 CHA: 0
Feathered Grey Robots with Giant Eyes: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have grey feathers. They have bilateral symmetry. Their giant eyes take up most of their head. They are humorless and believe in the inherent superiority of their species. They were created by the Third Republic of Antoids and Catoids on Cymos V as servants in 1061.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 2 CHA: 1
Scaly Grey Antoids with Five-fold Symmetry: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have grey scales. They have five-fold symmetry. They are thrill-seeking and always willing to listen. They developed from Scaly Grey Antoids in 699.
	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: -1 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: -1
Four-Armed Grey Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have grey skin. They have four arms. They have bilateral symmetry. They are hyperactive and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They were created by the Second Church of Antoids and Trolloids on Sativex VI as servants in 1040.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: -3 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 1
Scaly Grey Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have grey scales. They have bilateral symmetry. They are thrill-seeking and always willing to listen. They first evolved on Bemup II in 483.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: 1 CHA: 1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE EMPIRE OF ANTOIDS AND ROBOTS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, advanced Empire of 4 planets, with 4 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
3 billion Scaly Grey Antoids.
1 billion enslaved Four-Armed Grey Robots.
It is at war with the Second Church of Antoids and Trolloids.
It is at peace with the Third Republic of Antoids and Catoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: -3 DEX: -4 CON: -5 INT: -4 CHA: -6
THE SECOND CHURCH OF ANTOIDS AND TROLLOIDS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Church of 6 planets, with 32 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
4 billion Scaly Grey Antoids with Five-fold Symmetry.
22 billion Scaly Grey Antoids.
1 billion enslaved Four-Armed Robots with Giant Eyes.
4 billion enslaved Tiny Red Robots.
1 billion enslaved Feathered Grey Robots with Giant Eyes.
It is at war with the Empire of Antoids and Robots.
It is at peace with the Third Republic of Antoids and Catoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 0 CHA: -2
THE THIRD REPUBLIC OF ANTOIDS AND CATOIDS:
An ancient, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Republic of 11 planets, with 39 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
6 billion Scaly Grey Antoids with Five-fold Symmetry.
29 billion Scaly Grey Antoids.
4 billion enslaved Tiny Red Robots.
It controls a Universal Nutrient.
It is at peace with the Empire of Antoids and Robots.
It is at peace with the Second Church of Antoids and Trolloids.

	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 0 CON: -1 INT: 0 CHA: -2

In orbit: The insane space probe Mar'er threatening the planet.

Lifeforms of note:
Beautiful flying creatures: Fluttering fliers that display a dazzling array of colours.
Radiovores: These small worm-like creatures derive their energy directly from exposed deposits of radioactive materials.
Ultravores: The ultimate apex predator, the Ultravore is capable of stalking and killing even the most intelligent and well-armed prey.
